Our market-leading speech recognition accuracy rate enables Knovvu Virtual Agent to effectively automate simple tasks, help increase self-service and decrease costs for customer service operations.\n\nKnovvu Analytics \nKnovvu Analytics collect 100% of customer interaction data at customer service channels and convert it into meaningful information for decision-makers. The solution provides critical insights to understand customers better and help to improve their experiences. Equipped with advanced quality management tools, Knovvu Analytics enable supervisors to objectively score and maximize agent performance with tangible feedback\n\nKnovvu Biometrics \nMonitoring more than 100 unique parameters of the voice, Knovvu Biometrics can authorize callers within seconds. Being a language, accent, or content independent, it provides a seamless experience in real-time.","numberOfEmployees":{"value":200,"@type":"QuantitativeValue"},"logo":{"contentUrl":"https://media.licdn.com/dms/image/v2/D4D0BAQFh9Gt61ISGTQ/company-logo_200_200/B4DZT..OQUHYAM-/0/1739444512270/sestek_logo?e=2147483647&v=beta&t=NLRuRMqvqhM_VzJycKt72QuA9vW67g20tP8-xKZSuS4","description":"SESTEK","@type":"ImageObject"},"slogan":"Conversational automation company with 25 years of voice tech expertise, develops products under the brand name Knovvu","sameAs":"http://www.sestek.com"}]}

    <section class="core-section-container
        core-section-container--with-border border-b-1 border-solid border-color-border-faint py-4 text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us">
<!---->
          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              SESTEK is a conversational automation company working on AI-powered solutions for customer service since 2000. Our R&amp;D team of 100+ engineers develops conversational products built on technologies such as speech recognition (SR), natural language processing (NLP), and voice biometrics. We help digitize customer service operations of 500+ enterprise clients in 20 different countries around the globe.

SESTEK was acquired by Unifonic, one of the leading Communications Platform as a Service (CPaaS) providers, in 2022.

OUR PRODUCTS
Knovvu Virtual Agent
With 100% in-house developed Speech Recognition (SR) and Natural Language Understanding (NLU) technologies, Knovvu Virtual Agent understands customer intent and responds without the need for live agents. Our market-leading speech recognition accuracy rate enables Knovvu Virtual Agent to effectively automate simple tasks, help increase self-service and decrease costs for customer service operations.

Knovvu Analytics 
Knovvu Analytics collect 100% of customer interaction data at customer service channels and convert it into meaningful information for decision-makers. The solution provides critical insights to understand customers better and help to improve their experiences. Equipped with advanced quality management tools, Knovvu Analytics enable supervisors to objectively score and maximize agent performance with tangible feedback

Knovvu Biometrics 
Monitoring more than 100 unique parameters of the voice, Knovvu Biometrics can authorize callers within seconds. Being a language, accent, or content independent, it provides a seamless experience in real-time.
          </p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🌟 Celebrating 25 Years of SESTEK 🌟
 
This year marks a remarkable milestone: SESTEK turns 25!
 
Since 2000, we’ve been on a mission to transform speech and AI into smarter, more natural customer experiences. Along this journey, we’ve:
 
Introduced the first Agentic AI in contact centers
 
Pioneered Conversational Analytics for deeper customer insights
 
Launched Virtual Agent for seamless, multilingual, 24/7 interactions
 
These achievements were only possible thanks to the dedication of our team, the trust of our customers, and the support of our partners. 💙
 
Looking ahead, we remain committed to sustainable growth, advancing AI-driven solutions, and shaping the future of conversational automation.
 
✨ Here’s to the next 25 years of innovation, collaboration, and impact!

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Türkiye’s Pioneering Voice Enabled Agentic AI Technology is Live — Powered by <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/beko-corporate?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Beko Corporate</a> &amp; SESTEK

We’re proud to announce the deployment of Türkiye’s pioneering Voice Enabled Agentic AI Technology in Beko's contact center.

Knovvu Virtual Agent with Agentic AI is now live on the cloud, delivering human-like communication and customer care, handling 50,000+ calls monthly and managing installation appointment requests for 46 products across 10 Beko brands.

The process is fully automated with product-specific scenarios:  

✅ Confirms product-specific installation readiness through conversation
✅ Collects address and contact information 
✅ Aligns with customer availability
✅ Schedules appointments at the most suitable time slot

This milestone is a pioneer for Türkiye, setting a new benchmark in customer experience and service automation.
We’re proud to lead this innovation with <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/beko-corporate?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Beko Corporate</a>, delivering smarter, faster, and more seamless AI-driven experiences for customers.
 </p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🚀 Excited to announce the launch of our ITEA project <a class="link" href="https://in.linkedin.com/company/themedgpt?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>MedGPT</a> (Medical GPT: Revolutionizing Healthcare with Ethical AI)!

We are proud to contribute to the development of an AI-powered virtual assistant to support patients with pediatric diabetes and comorbidities — enabling more personalized and intuitive care.

The project is led by the Netherlands, with partners from Portugal, Turkey, and Austria 🌍 MedGPT will deliver an ethical, GenAI-powered medical assistant to make healthcare more proactive, customized, and efficient for both patients and professionals.</p>
